< review>
Platinum Collision Repair exceeded my expectations which is hard to do. PCC provided me a level of customer service from like the good old days when life was so much more simpler. From my first call I was treated like a V.I.P. They had their own tow service pick up my Model S Tesla promptly and from there on it was like I was staying at a 5 star hotel. When I arrived  I walked through the service stalls to the reception...backwards through a shop really. Most companies today due to liabilities would not allow a customer to walk through its shop floor. Anyway, the shop was so  extra clean you could practically eat off the floor. When we made it to the receptionist at the front of the building I was offered refreshments, water soda, coffee...really! I was then introduced to Crystal, my personal service support staff.
In the four weeks I worked with Crystal it was like being the CEO of a large company and she was my personal administrative assistant. Crystal handled every detail from working with Tesla Corporation for parts to my insurance company over budgets. She was always one step a head of me in communicating repair  status.
Check this out.  My insurance budgeted for used parts since my car was nearly six years old. PCC charged my insurance company only for used parts, but installed new OEM parts for me at the same price!
When I picked up the car (BTW mintly detailed to perfection) I got a walk around from Jan, one of the managers. Honestly, he gave me the time and attention as if I was part of his family. He showed me pictures on his cell phone on the progress of the repairs to my car! You would have thought it was his car not mine!! He took the time to educate me on all the meticulous details that went into fixing my ‚ÄúBaby.‚Äù I so appreciated the education and the special attention. Thank you Jan and Crystal and for the entire PCC staff for an amazing, headache free experience.

<Review>The service, professionalism and care at Platinum Collision Center were all superb.  The entire staff, from the receptionist to the owner (Tom), consistently provided excellent service beyond my expectations.

I had a minor fender-bender on my Tesla and needed to have the rear bumper repaired.
The estimate process was quick and easy.  Jackie meets you at the front desk in the most friendly and helpful manner.  Veronica assesses the damage thoroughly and provides the estimate.  They set up an immediate date for my repair and even made arrangements for me to get  a rental car at the site.  All I had to do was drop off my car.

Jhann, the manager, keeps you informed about the entire repair process.  He is very knowledgeable and experienced.  He works with the insurance company to get the repairs covered and completed as quickly as possible.  When my insurance company, State Farm, became less than willing to cover the necessary repairs, Jhann effectively communicated with me and State Farm to explain each itemized cost. < rating>
3</rating>
< review>
I got to the Amigo Room around 9 p.m. and it was rather inviting. I liked the decor and the vibe. It's a small space, but the booth setup provided what felt like a little privacy that allowed for talking with friends. Until a little later that hour when the DJ started. The volume was up so high that talking (or hearing anyway) became very difficult. I would anticipate that at a bar more suited to dancing, but the Amigo Room is more of a tiny, low-key, pseudo-Mexican cocktail bar that would be better left to those who want to sit and drink. However, that being said, it's not a great place to go if you appreciate a good drink. I was warned by more the one person in the party we were joining not to order the drinks that they had chosen, and my whiskey sour was all sour and nearly no whiskey. Overall, the Amigo Room had some charm, but probably not enough to get me back there.</review>

<date>1564714335873</date><Rate>5<//Rate>< text>
This is a place I have been to many times before, but not recently. I write this now because there is a new sheriff in town and he did time at Mikkeller DTLA. He scrapped the previous, anemic tap list and immediately installed the real deal on tap. I had a English pale from Yorkshire Square in Torrance and a Reissdorf Kolsch - an actual Kolsch from Cologne, fresh! This may easily be the new king in town when it comes to craft beer (not that that is saying much, unfortunately) and there are plans for more. Keep it up!</text>

This is the small version of Whole Foods hence the name Small Foods.... i'm kidding but not really.

It's like the size of one section of Whole Foods concentrated on selling snacks, small packaged items, bottled beverages, fresh food/sandwiches/salads, and fresh coffee and tea.

I only go here to get a cup of coffee or buy a bottled beverage. They have the high quality, organic, unique, and good for you beverages. Great shop to pick up a quick snack or drink!< /Text>

<Name>Jack Whyte<//Name><time>1498251229684< /time><Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
A real gem. Just because a new Blue Bottle outlet has opened next door, don't overlook Small Foods. Most of the store is a healthy grocery outlet, including lots of lunch options, but the front is all Cafe. The coffee isn't quite Blue Bottle standard, but it's very close, and it's a little less pretentious proto-hipster (plus the lines are far shorter). The staff are awesome, especially the dude with two-tone hair who clearly has amazing taste in music. Coffee and croissant, with early Pink Floyd blasting out, is as San Francisco as it gets. No Wifi though, so don't expect to be productive.</text>

< Review>
I know I shouldn't shop at Small Foods, because everything is very pricey here, but the convenience of it makes it hard to resist.

I probably come here 3-4 times a week during my lunch breaks. The crowd is your usual SOMA crowd. They have a great selection of salads and sandwiches at their deli counter. I try to avoid the sushi because premade sushi tends to be awful, and this place is no exception.

The staff tends to be generally friendly, although you'll occasionally run across a very grumpy barista.

Overall, I'd recommend coming here for a quick bite or to pick up some flowers if needed. They used to have a wider assortment, but now it's all supplied by Farmgirl Flowers.</Review>
